     <p>In order to force specific layouts, use the <code class="prettyprint">HYPE_eventListeners</code> infrastructure to listen to “HypeLayoutRequest” events and return a different layout name from the callback. </p> 
     <h2 id="timeline-functions">Timeline Functions</h2> 
     <p><a name="startTimelineNamed"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-starttimelinenamed39timelinename39-directioncode"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.startTimelineNamed('timelineName', direction)</code></h4> 
     <p>Starts the specified timeline at the beginning for the current scene. Note: timelines are user-defined, so they are not enforced to be unique. If you are going to use this function, be sure that no two timelines in any scene have the same name!</p> 
     <p>Direction to play timeline:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionForward</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionReverse</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p>Note: this function was named <span class="codesnippet">hypeDocument.playTimelineNamed(timelineName)</span> in <span class="notranslate">Tumult Hype</span> 1.5 and earlier. </p> 
     <p><a name="pauseTimelineNamed"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-pausetimelinenamed39timelinename39code"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.pauseTimelineNamed('timelineName')</code></h4> 
     <p>Pauses the specified timeline for the current scene.</p> 
     <p><a name="continueTimelineNamed"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-continuetimelinenamedtimelinename-direction-canrestarttimelinecode"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.continueTimelineNamed(timelineName, direction, canRestartTimeline)</code></h4> 
     <p>Continues the specified timeline in the direction specified where it left off for the current scene. Note: timelines are user-defined, so they are not enforced to be unique. If you are going to use this function, be sure that no two timelines in any scene have the same name!</p> 
     <p>By default, continue will not start the timeline over if it is at the end. To change this behavior pass <code class="prettyprint">true</code> for <code class="prettyprint">canRestartTimeline</code>.</p> 
     <p>Direction to play timeline:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionForward</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionReverse</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p>An example that plays the Main Timeline of the current scene in the forward direction and will start the timeline over if the end has already been reached: <code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.continueTimelineNamed('Main Timeline', hypeDocument.kDirectionForward, true)</code></p> 
     <p><a name="goToTimeInTimelineNamed"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-gototimeintimelinenamedtimeinseconds-39timelinename39code"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.goToTimeInTimelineNamed(timeInSeconds, 'timelineName')</code></h4> 
     <p>Jumps to a specific time in the specified timeline for the current scene.</p> 
     <h4 style="display:none;" id="currentTimeInTimelineNamed">.</h4> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-currenttimeintimelinenamed39timelinename39code"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.currentTimeInTimelineNamed('timelineName')</code></h4> 
     <p>Returns the current time of the specified timeline in seconds.</p> 
     <p><a name="durationForTimelineNamed"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-durationfortimelinenamed39timelinename39code"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.durationForTimelineNamed('timelineName')</code></h4> 
     <p>Returns the duration of the specified timeline in seconds.</p> 
     <p><a name="currentDirectionForTimelineNamed"></a> </p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-currentdirectionfortimelinenamed39timelinename39code"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.currentDirectionForTimelineNamed('timelineName')</code></h4> 
     <p>Returns the playback direction of the specified timeline. </p> 
     <p>Possible return values:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionForward</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionReverse</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p><a name="isPlayingTimelineNamed"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprinthypedocument-isplayingtimelinenamed39timelinename39code"><code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.isPlayingTimelineNamed('timelineName')</code></h4> 
     <p>Returns true if the timeline is playing and false if it is not.</p> 
     <p></p>
     <aside class="notice">
      <p></p> 
      <p>Timeline names are user-defined and uniqueness is not enforced. If you are going to use these functions, be sure that no two timelines in any scene have the same name.</p> 
      <p></p>
     </aside>
     <p></p> 
     <h2 id="symbol-functions">Symbol Functions</h2> 
     <p>For an explanation of Symbols jump to the <a href="#symbols">Symbols</a> documentation chapter.</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="getSymbolInstanceById">hypeDocument.getSymbolInstanceById(id)</h4> 
     <p>Returns the symbolInstance for the symbol with the specified id.<br><br>The symbol instance can be used to control timelines in the symbol. See the Symbol Instances section for more information.</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="getSymbolInstancesByName"> hypeDocument.getSymbolInstancesByName(symbolName) </h4> 
     <p>Returns all symbolInstances with the specified name. A symbol’s name can be found in the Symbol Library. The symbol instance can be used to control timelines in the symbol. See the Symbol Instances section for more information.</p> 
     <h2 id="symbol-instances">Symbol Instances</h2> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="getSymbolInstancesByNameSymbol">symbolInstance.getSymbolInstancesByName(symbolName) </h4> 
     <p>Returns all symbolInstances with the specified name that are children of symbolInstance.element(). A symbol’s name can be found in the Symbol Library.</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="symbolName">symbolInstance.symbolName()</h4> 
     <p>Returns the name of the symbol.</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="element-symbol">symbolInstance.element()</h4> 
     <p>Returns the element representing the symbol.</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="startTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.startTimelineNamed(timelineName, direction)</h4> 
     <p>Starts the specified timeline at the beginning for the symbol. Note: timelines are user-defined, so they are not enforced to be unique. If you are going to use this function, be sure that no two timelines in the symbol have the same name!</p> 
     <p>Direction to play timeline:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionForward</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionReverse</span>
</code></pre> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="pauseTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.pauseTimelineNamed(timelineName)</h4> 
     <p>Pauses the specified timeline for the symbol. Note: timelines are user-defined, so they are not enforced to be unique. If you are going to use this function, be sure that no two timelines in the symbol have the same name!</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="continueTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.continueTimelineNamed(timelineName, direction)</h4> 
     <p>Continues the specified timeline where it left off for the symbol. Note: timelines are user-defined, so they are not enforced to be unique. If you are going to use this function, be sure that no two timelines in the symbol have the same name!</p> 
     <p>Direction to play timeline:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionForward</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionReverse</span>
</code></pre> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="goToTimeInTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.goToTimeInTimelineNamed(timeInSeconds, timelineName)</h4> 
     <p>Jumps to a specific time in the specified timeline for the symbol. Note: timelines are user-defined, so they are not enforced to be unique. If you are going to use this function, be sure that no two timelines in the symbol have the same name!</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="currentTimeInTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.currentTimeInTimelineNamed(timelineName)</h4> 
     <p>Returns the current time of the specified timeline in seconds.</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="durationForTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.durationForTimelineNamed(timelineName)</h4> 
     <p>Returns the duration of the specified timeline in seconds.</p> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="currentDirectionForTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.currentDirectionForTimelineNamed(timelineName)</h4> 
     <p>Returns the playback direction of the specified timeline. </p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionForward</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kDirectionReverse</span>
</code></pre> 
     <h4 class="notranslate" id="isPlayingTimelineNamedSymbol">symbolInstance.isPlayingTimelineNamed(timelineName)</h4> 
     <p>Returns true if the timeline is playing and false if it is not.</p> 
     <p>Explore tips and tricks in the <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/c/symbols">Symbols section of the forums</a>. </p> 
     <h2 id="dragapi">Drag Functions</h2> 
     <p>JavaScript functions invoked by the On Drag handler can gather information about the current drag gesture. </p> 
     <p><a name="hypegesturephase"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprintevent39hypegesturephase39code"><code class="prettyprint">event['hypeGesturePhase']</code></h4> 
     <p>When receiving a callback for the On Drag event with the Run Javascript… action the event object also offers information about whether the current drag gesture has just started or ended, was canceled, or the coordinates were updated. To get that state, access the hypeGesturePhase property in the event object:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kHypeGesturePhaseStart</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kHypeGesturePhaseMove</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kHypeGesturePhaseEnd</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kHypeGesturePhaseCancel</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p><a name="hypegesturexposition"></a> </p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprintevent39hypegesturexposition39code"><code class="prettyprint">event['hypeGestureXPosition']</code></h4> 
     <p>Returns the current x position of a drag when using the “On Drag” event with the “Run Javascript…” action.</p> 
     <p><a name="hypegestureyposition"></a></p> 
     <h4 id="code-classprettyprintevent39hypegestureyposition39code"><code class="prettyprint">event['hypeGestureYPosition']</code></h4> 
     <p>Returns the current y position of a drag when using the “On Drag” event with the “Run Javascript…” action.</p> 
     <p></p>
     <aside class="note">
       Using the X and Y position events above allows you to create draggable elements constrained within a defined area. 
      <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/t/drag-element-limited-by-container-without-additional-js-library/1349">Example here</a>.
     </aside>
     <p></p> 
     <h2 id="api-constants">API Constants</h2> 
     <p>The only constants exposed are those for scene transitions:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kSceneTransitionInstant</span>  
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kSceneTransitionCrossfade</span>  
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kSceneTransitionSwap</span>  
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kSceneTransitionPushLeftToRight</span>  
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kSceneTransitionPushRightToLeft</span>  
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kSceneTransitionPushBottomToTop</span>  
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">kSceneTransitionPushTopToBottom</span>  
</code></pre>
     <h3 id="examples">Examples</h3> 
     <p>To show a scene named “Yellow” with the Instant transition style, this API function call would be used:</p> 
     <p>hypeDocument.showSceneNamed(‘Yellow’);</p> 
     <p>To show a specific scene named “Blue” from the JavaScript editor, using a Push Right to Left transition, and then play a timeline named “Robin” these function calls would be used:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">showSceneNamed</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'Blue'</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">kSceneTransitionPushRightToLeft</span><span class="p">);</span>
<span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">playTimelineNamed</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'Robin'</span><span class="p">);</span>
</code></pre>
     <h2 id="invoking-api-from-outside-oftumult-hype">Invoking API from outside of&nbsp;Tumult Hype</h2> 
     <p>To access the&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;API from a JavaScript outside of the embedded document, you can use the global&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;object:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nx">HYPE</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">documents</span><span class="p">[</span><span class="nx">documentName</span><span class="p">]</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p>The document may not be an exact match for the filename. To figure out the value, you can look inside the exported Resources folder for the *_hype_generated_script.js file and find the document’s name there. You can also call the&nbsp;hypeDocument.documentName()&nbsp;function from within a JavaScript action to determine it.</p> 
     <h3 id="events">Events</h3> 
     <p>To help external JavaScripts integrate and interact with embedded documents&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;offers an event callback system, allowing external JavaScript functions to be triggered in response to events in embedded documents. One purpose for an externally invoked event would be to jump between scenes using controls outside of your&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;document for a slideshow. At this time, four event callbacks are offered, so functions can be registered for document loading, scene loading and unloading, and timeline completion:</p> 
     <p>HypeDocumentLoad<br> HypeSceneLoad<br> HypeSceneUnload<br> HypeTimelineComplete </p> 
     <p>The&nbsp;HypeTimelineComplete&nbsp;event also adds a&nbsp;name&nbsp;property to the event object, so you can determine which timeline raised the event.</p> 
     <h3 id="examples">Examples</h3> 
     <p>The following example registers an event to be run after the&nbsp;<code class="prettyprint">HypeDocumentLoad</code>&nbsp;event has occurred:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight html"><code><span class="nt">&lt;script&gt;</span>

  <span class="kd">function</span> <span class="nx">myCallback</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">element</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="c1">// display the name of the Hype container and the event called</span>
    <span class="nx">alert</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"id: "</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="nx">element</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">id</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="s2">" type: "</span> <span class="o">+</span> <span class="nx">event</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">type</span><span class="p">);</span>

    <span class="c1">// show the scene named SecondScene</span>
    <span class="nx">hypeDocument</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">showSceneNamed</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s1">'SecondScene'</span><span class="p">);</span>

    <span class="c1">// return false so it does not load the initial scene</span>
    <span class="k">return</span> <span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">;</span>
  <span class="p">}</span>

  <span class="k">if</span><span class="p">(</span><span class="s2">"HYPE_eventListeners"</span> <span class="k">in</span> <span class="nb">window</span> <span class="o">===</span> <span class="kc">false</span><span class="p">)</span> <span class="p">{</span>
    <span class="nb">window</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">HYPE_eventListeners</span> <span class="o">=</span> <span class="nb">Array</span><span class="p">();</span>
  <span class="p">}</span>
  <span class="nb">window</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">HYPE_eventListeners</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">push</span><span class="p">({</span><span class="s2">"type"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="s2">"HypeDocumentLoad"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">"callback"</span><span class="p">:</span><span class="nx">myCallback</span><span class="p">});</span>

 <span class="nt">&lt;/script&gt;</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p>The following line in the above JavaScript receives the&nbsp; HypeDocumentLoad&nbsp;event callback:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight javascript"><code><span class="nb">window</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">HYPE_eventListeners</span><span class="p">.</span><span class="nx">push</span><span class="p">({</span><span class="s2">"type"</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="s2">"HypeDocumentLoad"</span><span class="p">,</span> <span class="s2">"callback"</span> <span class="p">:</span> <span class="nx">myCallback</span><span class="p">});</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p>In the above code,&nbsp;<code class="prettyprint">HypeDocumentLoad</code>&nbsp;is the event for which the callback should be triggered, and&nbsp;<code class="prettyprint">myCallback</code>&nbsp;is the JavaScript function which should be invoked by the event. This JavaScript can be invoked outside of&nbsp;Tumult Hype, and can potentially be placed within the&nbsp;<code class="prettyprint">&lt;head&gt;...&lt;/head&gt;</code>&nbsp;of the exported .html file generated by&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;by clicking on ‘Edit HTML Head’ in the Document Inspector. To see this function in action, download&nbsp;<a href="https://tumult.com/hype/documentation/3.0/documents/ExternalEvent.hype.zip">this example file</a>. When previewed in a browser, the code in the document’s head will load the second scene and an additional timeline on that scene.</p> 
     <p>These buttons make use of&nbsp;Tumult Hype’s&nbsp;<a href="#apiconstants">JavaScript API constants</a>. The full code for the Push Right to Left button is:&nbsp; </p> 
     <pre class="highlight html"><code><span class="nt">&lt;button</span> <span class="na">type=</span><span class="s">"button"</span> <span class="na">onclick =</span><span class="s">"HYPE.documents['scenes-transitions'].showSceneNamed('Scene2',HYPE.documents['scenes-transitions'].kSceneTransitionPushRightToLeft);"</span><span class="nt">&gt;</span>
   Show Scene 2 (Push Right to Left)
 <span class="nt">&lt;/button&gt;</span>
</code></pre> 
     <p>Switch to a scene named Red from a document named HypeExample using the Push Right to Left transition:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight html"><code><span class="nt">&lt;a</span> <span class="na">href=</span><span class="s">"#"</span> <span class="na">onclick=</span><span class="s">"HYPE.documents['HypeExample'].showSceneNamed('Red',HYPE.documents['HypeExample'].kSceneTransitionPushRightToLeft);"</span><span class="nt">&gt;</span>Go to the Red Scene.<span class="nt">&lt;/a&gt;</span> 
</code></pre> 
     <p>Switch to the next scene in a document named HypeExample using the Crossfade transition:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight html"><code><span class="nt">&lt;a</span> <span class="na">href=</span><span class="s">"#"</span> <span class="na">onclick=</span><span class="s">"HYPE.documents['HypeExample'].showNextScene(HYPE.documents['HypeExample'].kSceneTransitionCrossfade);"</span><span class="nt">&gt;</span>Crossfade to next Scene<span class="nt">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.
</code></pre> 
     <p></p>
     <aside class="notice">
      Note: Because the&nbsp;HYPE&nbsp;global variable may not be available immediately after HTML document has been loaded, this is the only reliable way to trigger external JavaScript functions in response to an embedded&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;document being loaded.
     </aside>
     <p></p> 
     <h2 id="javascript-forums">JavaScript Forums</h2> 
     <p>The <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/c/javascript">JavaScript category</a> of the Tumult forums contains a wide assortment of code samples and example documents. The <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/t/hype-extension-project-post-extensions-here/6847?u=daniel">Hype Extension Project</a>, for example, covers several powerful functions to extend <span class="notranslate">Tumult Hype’s</span> functionality with the help of the JavaScript API.</p> 
     <h1 id="inspectors">Inspectors</h1> 
     <p>Tumult Hype’s nine inspectors provide easy access to document, symbol, scene, element, typography, physics, and identity properties.</p> 
     <p>Inspectors are accessible from the View menu, or by clicking the Inspector toolbar button. Document and Scene inspectors establish rules and settings for the document and scene. The Metrics, Element, Symbol, Text, Mouse Action, and Identity inspectors become active when selecting one or more elements or symbols. Tumult Hype Pro includes two additional inspectors to modify symbol and physics properties.</p> 
     <h2 id="document-inspector">Document Inspector</h2> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector35Document.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector35Document@2x.png" width="275" height="817" alt=""></p> 
     <p>The Document inspector provides many controls for initial document setup.</p> 
     <p><strong>HTML Page Title</strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;Defines the title of the exported HTML document. By default, the title is the same as the exported file name.</p> 
     <p><strong>Options</strong></p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Show Loading Indicator</strong>&nbsp;– Controls the display of a loading indicator. When enabled, the&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;document will display “Loading…” as the document’s image resources are downloaded and cached. For tips on customizing the preloading screen, please read our support article on <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/t/creating-a-custom-preloader/1343">Custom Preloaders</a>. </li> 
      <li><strong>Make Background Transparent</strong> – When selected, scene backgrounds are transparent. Check this box to export transparent animated gifs. </li> 
      <li><p><strong>Create offline application cache</strong>&nbsp;– When selected,&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;generates a cache manifest file for resources used in your project. With this option selected, your document, when loaded as a web app, will download and locally save everything needed to ensure the document works even when the device is offline.&nbsp;<strong>Note:</strong>&nbsp;Your document will need to be loaded once as a web app to prime the cache. Also, Google fonts require an Internet connection as they cannot be cached on the device.</p></li> 
      <li><p><strong>Edit the Head HTML</strong>&nbsp;– Clicking this button opens an HTML editor, allowing the editing of the document’s <code class="prettyprint">&lt;head&gt;</code>. Any changes made to the document’s header are represented in&nbsp;Tumult Hype’s scene editor and are also included when the document is exported.</p></li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><strong>Advanced Options</strong></p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Protect from External Styles</strong> - When unchecked, elements will not be protected from CSS styles defined outside of your Tumult Hype document. </li> 
      <li><strong>Use Webkit Graphics Acceleration</strong>&nbsp;– When selected, animations can use the system’s GPU when displayed in Webkit-based browsers, which includes Safari, Mobile Safari, and Chrome. This almost always leads to better animation performance, but some browsers or devices may have problems properly rendering accelerated content. If you see rendering problems, try deselecting this option.</li> 
      <li><strong>Position with CSS left/top</strong> - When checked, elements animate using CSS’s left &amp; top values. Check this box if you are manipulating element positions directly with JavaScript or with Jquery. </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><strong>Mobile Options</strong>&nbsp;– These options set properties on the exported .html page</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Viewport</strong>&nbsp;– Choosing Document Width sets the document’s viewport to match your document’s width. Device Width and Device Height define the exported document’s viewport to match the viewing screen’s width or height. Choosing Don’t Set excludes any viewport tag from your document’s exported content.</li> 
      <li><strong>Initial Scale 1.0</strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;Selecting this option adds the “initial-scale=1.0” property to the exported page’s viewport.</li> 
      <li><strong>Allow user scaling</strong>&nbsp;– When selected, users can pinch and zoom to zoom in to and out of your document.</li> 
      <li><strong>Use touch events</strong>&nbsp;– When selected, actions set in the Actions inspector default to tap events when possible. For example, a Mouse Click will be fired after a Tap without any delay.</li> 
      <li><strong>Home screen web app</strong>&nbsp;– This option allows visitors to add your web app to their iOS device’s home screen and choose a color for the status bar. To add the Apple Touch Startup images to your document,&nbsp;<a href="#appleimages">click here</a>.</li> 
      <li><strong>Status bar</strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;If “Home screen web app” is enabled, allows you to choose the desired appearance for your web app’s status bar.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><strong>Show Browser Compatibility Warnings</strong>&nbsp;– Warnings for browsers equal to or older than the selected version will be shown. Changing settings here will not affect document compatibility, only the warnings reported by&nbsp;Tumult Hype. Documents created with&nbsp;Tumult Hype always have the best possible compatibility with all browsers. Use the <a href="#advanced-export">Advanced Export</a> feature to turn off IE compatibility. </p> 
     <h2 id="scene-inspector">Scene Inspector</h2> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector35Scene.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector35Scene@2x.png" width="274" height="917" alt=""></p> 
     <p><strong>Document Size</strong></p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Preset Sizes</strong>&nbsp;– Contains many commonly used default document sizes for mobile devices, iBooks widgets, IAB default advertising sizes, and publishing platforms. </li> 
      <li><strong>Width and Height</strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;Control over the exact width and height of the document, in pixels. The scene size adjusts the size of all scenes unless ‘Apply changes to all scenes’ is unchecked. - Use a percentage-based width or height to use <a href="#flexible-layout">Flexible Layouts</a></li> 
      <li><strong>Scale</strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;Controls whether the document should scale horizontally and/or vertically. When enabled, the controls offer the ability to specify how much of the containing window or div the Hype document should expand to fill. See the&nbsp;<a href="#flexible-layout/">Flexible Layout Chapter</a>&nbsp;to learn more.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><strong>Responsive Layout</strong></p> 
     <p>By default, scenes only have one layout that layout is always displayed regardless of the browser’s width. To take advantage of Hype Pro’s responsive layouts, click the Add New Layout button and add layouts as desired. The “Breakpoint width” field is used to control which layout is displayed for a given browser width. Read more about <a href="#responsive-layouts">Responsive Layouts</a>. </p> 
     <p><strong>Breakpoint width</strong> - Sets the breakpoint width of the current responsive layout.</p> 
     <p><strong>Add New Layout…</strong> - Adds an additional layout. </p> 
     <p><strong>Animation Timelines</strong></p> 
     <p>This area displays the timelines on the current scene, their duration, and toggles whether timelines are relative or absolute. (<a href="#absolute-and-relative-keyframes">Learn more about relative and absolute timelines</a>. Add timelines to the current scene by clicking the Plus button; remove them by clicking the Minus button. Rename timelines by double clicking on their name.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Background</strong> – Sets the background color of the current scene. Scene colors set on the first scene sets the background color of the exported .html file.</li> 
      <li><strong>Scene Actions</strong> – Please see the <a href="#actions">Actions</a> chapter for more information.</li> 
      <li><strong>Custom Behaviors</strong> - The “Add new behavior” button creates new <a href="#behaviors">custom behaviors</a>.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <h2 id="symbol-inspector">Symbol Inspector</h2> 
     <p><a href="http://tumult.com/hype/pro" alt="Learn More" title="Learn More" class="profeature">HYPE PRO ONLY<br></a></p>
     <div class="profeaturebottom"></div>
     <p></p> 
     <p>Hype replaces the Scene inspector with the Symbol inspector when you are actively editing a symbol’s content. Double click a symbol to enter editing mode and display this inspector.</p> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector35Symbol.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector35Symbol@2x.png" width="270" height="611" alt=""></p> 
     <h3 id="type">Type</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Standard</strong> - Standard symbols can have multiple instances in a scene and exist within the scene itself just as normal elements do.</li> 
      <li><strong>Persistent</strong> - Persistent symbols can only exist once on a scene and, unlike elements or standard symbols, exist outside of scenes. As such, they are not destroyed when scenes change, and can even be displayed while a scene transition happens. 
       <ul> 
        <li><strong>Automatically add to new scenes</strong> - New scenes will contain the selected persistent symbol when the scene is created.</li> 
        <li><strong>Display on top during scene transition</strong>: No matter the layer order of the symbol, it will appear above all elements during scene transitions.</li> 
       </ul></li> 
     </ul> 
     <h2 id="metrics-inspector">Metrics Inspector</h2> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector35Metrics.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector35Metrics@2x.png" width="273" height="788" alt=""></p> 
     <p>The Metrics inspector controls size, content overflow behavior, placement, and rotation properties of selected elements. While rotation, position, and scaling can all be manipulated directly in the scene area with mouse controls, this inspector offers fine tuning and may be more useful during multiple selection.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Content Overflow</strong>&nbsp;– Determines how text and inner elements are displayed when it extends beyond the bounds of the element, and whether a scroll bar should appear. </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><strong>Placement</strong></p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Left, top, Width &amp; Height</strong>&nbsp;– Sets the exact height, width, and position for the selected elements. </li> 
      <li><strong>Constrain Proportions</strong> - Ensures elements scale proportionally when resizing. </li> 
      <li><strong>Original Size</strong> - Returns element to their original size. </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><strong>Scale</strong> </p> 
     <p>Scales up or down the selected selected element(s) or group. This uses CSS’s transform:scale() property.“ Setting negative values in either dimension will flip the element. To scale width or height independently, uncheck Constrain ratio. To reset scale to 100%, click the Original Size button. </p> 
     <p><strong>Flexible Layout</strong>&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> 
     <p>Selecting and deselecting the pins and scaling arrows define how selected elements should behave as the exported Hype document is resized. For more information, please see the&nbsp;<a href="https://tumult.com/hype/documentation/flexible-layout/">Flexible Layout</a>&nbsp;chapter.</p> 
     <p><strong>Scaling Behavior</strong>&nbsp;–&nbsp;Defines how elements should resize. In particular, offers control over how proportionally sized elements, like images, should be resized to preserve their aspect ratio.</p> 
     <p><strong>Rotation</strong>&nbsp;</p> 
     <p>Sets the X, Y, and Z rotation angles. At this time only one rotation angle may be selected at one time. Negative values like -180° or values exceeding 360° are accepted. For example, to set a new rotation value for three full rotations clockwise, use 1080°.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Rotation follows motion path</strong>&nbsp;– When selected, element will rotate with the direction of a motion path. Rotation angles may be applied in addition to this setting.</li> 
      <li><strong>Transform Origin</strong>&nbsp;– Sets the X and Y offset percentages for the selected element’s rotation and scale origin. This setting can also be adjusted by selecting an element, holding command, and adjusting the center point. </li> 
     </ul> 
     <h2 id="element-inspector">Element Inspector</h2> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector35Element.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector35Element@2x.png" width="276" height="875" alt=""></p> 
     <p>The Element inspector contains stylistic properties for the selected element or elements.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><p><strong>Background Fill Style</strong>&nbsp;– Sets the background style as either an Image, Fill, Gradient, or None.</p> 
       <ul> 
        <li>Gradients contain two colors (with or without alpha transparency) and may be rotated.</li> 
        <li>Images may be scaled to fit the element, repeated horizontally, or repeated vertically.</li> 
       </ul></li> 
      <li><p><strong>Border</strong>&nbsp;– Creates a border with the selected style (None, Solid, Double, Dotted, Dashed, Groove, Ridge, Inset, Outset) around the selected element. The border and radius of an element’s four sides and corners can be set in this panel, as well as the color and style of the border. The padding setting controls the distance between the border and the element.</p></li> 
      <li><p><strong>Visibility</strong>&nbsp;– A value of 0% opacity sets selected elements as completely invisible. Note: An element with a 0% opacity will interfere with mouse actions on elements ordered below it in the scene. For an element to respond to mouse actions at a region in the document, it must not be covered by any other element, visible or invisible, at that point.</p></li> 
      <li><p><strong>Display</strong> - Toggles the visibility of the selected element(s). </p></li> 
      <li><p><strong>Shadow</strong> - Simulates a box shadow of the selected element, with settings for its color, position, and blur radius amount.</p></li> 
      <li><p><strong>Filter Effects</strong>&nbsp;</p></li> 
     </ul> 
     <p>CSS3 filters perform a variety of powerful image rendering effects. <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/CSS/filter">Read more about these effects.</a></p> 
     <p><strong>Foreground</strong> - Setting values on foreground filter effects will modify the element’s blur, sepia, saturation, hue, brightness, or contrast. <strong>Backdrop</strong> - These properties define how elements underneath the selected element appear. Your element must have a opacity value under 1.0 to perceive these effects. Lower the opacity slider at the bottom of the color picker to add transparency to your element. <em>Note: Supported in iOS 9+ and Safari 9+</em> - <strong>Reflection</strong>&nbsp;– This property creates a reflection of the selected element, with optional depth and offset values.</p> 
     <h2 id="typography-inspector">Typography Inspector</h2> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/InspectorTypography.png" data-src-retina="images/InspectorTypography@2x.png" width="275" height="583" alt="Typography Inspector"> </p> 
     <p>The Typography inspector controls text formatting including font selection, colors, alignment, shadows and spacing properties.</p> 
     <p>By default, all fonts appear in the Font Family selection panel. The iOS font family option lists fonts installed on iOS devices. The Web option lists fonts installed on a majority of web browsers.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Alignment</strong>&nbsp;– The text alignment of the selected elements.</li> 
      <li><strong>Font</strong>&nbsp;– The Font Family, size and style of the selected elements.</li> 
      <li><strong>Add More Fonts</strong>: Loads the Google Fonts overlay to select fonts from Google’s <a href="http://www.google.com/fonts/">Font Directory</a>.</li> 
      <li><strong>Text Shadow</strong>&nbsp;– Sets a shadow for selected text with specified X, Y, blur radius, and color properties.</li> 
      <li><strong>Text Spacing</strong>&nbsp;– Letter spacing defines the distance between characters, word spacing defines the distance between words, and line height sets the distance between individual lines.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p>To add arbitrary HTML or CSS styles to a text element, edit its inner HTML by double clicking it and then clicking on the pencil icon which appears beneath the element.</p> 
     <p>For more information about Fonts, see the&nbsp;<a href="#typography">Typography</a>&nbsp;chapter.</p> 
     <h2 id="actions-inspector">Actions Inspector</h2> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector35Actions.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector35Actions@2x.png" width="271" height="535" alt="Actions Inspector"></p> 
     <p><strong>Pointer</strong> </p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Cursor</strong> - The Cursor setting controls how the user’s cursor should appear when mousing over the selected element. Mouse actions are explained in the <a href="#Actions">Actions</a> chapter of the documentation. </li> 
      <li><strong>Allow text selection</strong> - Disabling this ensures text in an element cannot be copied. </li> 
      <li><strong>Ignore all pointer events</strong> - Checking this box ensure that even if an element has be positioned over another element, the element below will receive mouse &amp; touch events. </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p>The actions listed occur based on what element or elements have been selected. </p> 
     <h2 id="physics-inspector">Physics Inspector</h2> 
     <p><a href="http://tumult.com/hype/pro" alt="Learn More" title="Learn More" class="profeature">HYPE PRO ONLY<br></a></p>
     <div class="profeaturebottom"></div>
     <p></p> 
     <p>The Physics Inspector controls physics properties of the selected elements or scene.</p> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector35Physics.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector35Physics@2x.png" width="275" height="336" alt=""></p> 
     <h3 id="element-physics">Element Physics</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Inactive - No physics applied</strong>: The element will not participate at all in physics. It is not affected by gravity, nor will it interact with other elements.</li> 
      <li><strong>Static - Interacts without movement</strong>: Gravity does not affect static elements. Static elements are useful for creating hard edges through which dynamic elements cannot pass.</li> 
      <li><strong>Dynamic - Full physics body</strong>: Gravity settings for the scene affect dynamic physics bodies on scene load. These elements will collide with other dynamic bodies and static bodies on the same scene.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <h3 id="physics-properties">Physics Properties</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Bounce</strong>: Controls the elasticity of the element’s collisions. A value of zero means the element is inelastic and will not bounce in a collision; the higher the value, the more the element will bounce.</li> 
      <li><strong>Friction</strong>: Sets the coefficient of friction for the element. A value of zero means the element will not slow down as it moves through the scene, while a higher value means it will slow more quickly as it moves.</li> 
      <li><strong>Density</strong>: Changes an element’s mass and thus how the element will affect other elements during a collision. Mass is determined by an element’s size and density. A larger, less dense element can have the same mass as a smaller, more dense element.</li> 
      <li><strong>Air Drag</strong>: The friction air provides when an object falls. A beach ball would have high air drag and a bowling ball low air drag.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <h3 id="scenesymbol-physics-gravity">Scene/Symbol Physics Gravity</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Force</strong>: Sets the strength of gravity in the scene or symbol. 1.0 is Earth-like.</li> 
      <li><strong>Angle</strong>: Controls the direction of gravity. The default value of 180° pulls affected elements to the bottom of the scene.</li> 
      <li><strong>Control gravity with device tilt</strong>: When enabled, the direction of gravity is controlled by the devices orientation angle so that tilting the device will change the direction of gravity.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <h2 id="identity-inspector">Identity Inspector</h2> 
     <p><img class="inspector" src="images/bg.png" data-src="images/Inspector36Identity.png" data-src-retina="images/Inspector36Identity@2x.png" width="277" height="420" alt="Identity Inspector"></p> 
     <p>The Identity inspector provides access to metadata for elements and information for screen reading technologies. To learn more about Accessibility options in Hype, read the <a href="#accessibility">Accessibility</a> chapter.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li><strong>Alternate Text&nbsp;</strong>– Sets the alt tag and accessibility title for images and the title tag for divs. Setting this value is useful for accessibility and for displaying tooltips.</li> 
      <li><strong>Include in keyboard Navigation</strong>- Sets the tab index value for the selected element.</li> 
      <li><strong>Display Name</strong>&nbsp;– Sets the element’s name in the element list.</li> 
      <li><strong>Unique Element ID</strong>&nbsp;– Sets the element’s ID for accessing the element directly in a custom function or JavaScript. Please see the&nbsp;<a href="#javascript">JavaScript</a>&nbsp;chapter for more details.</li> 
      <li><strong>Class Name</strong> - Sets a CSS class name for the element.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><strong>Example</strong>: A button with the ‘Alternate Text’ set to ‘Submit Button’, a ‘Tab Index’ value of 6, a Unique element id set to <code class="prettyprint">nextscene-button</code>, and a class name of <code class="prettyprint">button-lrg</code> will output the following HTML during export:</p> 
     <pre class="highlight html"><code><span class="nt">&lt;div</span> <span class="na">class=</span><span class="s">"HYPE_element button-lrg"</span> <span class="na">id=</span><span class="s">"nextscene-button"</span> <span class="na">title=</span><span class="s">"Next Scene"</span> <span class="na">alt=</span><span class="s">"Submit Button "</span> <span class="na">tabindex=</span><span class="s">"6"</span> <span class="na">role=</span><span class="s">"button"</span> <span class="na">style=</span><span class="s">"..."</span><span class="nt">&gt;</span>Next Scene<span class="nt">&lt;/div&gt;</span>
</code></pre>

     <h1 id="troubleshooting">Troubleshooting</h1> 
     <p>For general questions about Tumult Hype and pre-purchase questions, please <a href="http://tumult.com/hype/faq/">visit our FAQ</a>.</p> 
     <h2 id="browser-amp-document-issues">Browser &amp; Document Issues</h2> 
     <p><strong>Browser-Specific Issues</strong></p> 
     <p>Seeing an issue with your font in Firefox? A performance issue when you preview in Chrome? First, check the developer console of your browser to examine any potential console errors. Here’s how to enable your developer console in <a href="https://developers.google.com/web/tools/chrome-devtools/console/">Chrome</a>, <a href="https://developer.apple.com/library/content/documentation/AppleApplications/Conceptual/Safari_Developer_Guide/GettingStarted/GettingStarted.html">Safari</a>, and <a href="https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Tools/Web_Console/Opening_the_Web_Console">Firefox</a>. For an overview of how to test Tumult Hype documents in multiple browsers, <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/t/video-tutorials-testing-your-tumult-hype-documents-on-chrome-windows-ios-and-android/1381">visit this forum post</a>.</p> 
     <p>Developer consoles in browsers help you identify a number of issues: </p> 
     <ul> 
      <li>If an image is missing when previewing on the web and you see a ‘404’ error, it likely means that the image has not been uploaded to the server. </li> 
      <li>You can identify ‘computed’ css styles to help you identify display issues across browsers. For example, the line-height might appear different on Mobile Safari. </li> 
      <li>‘Undefined’ errors often occur when using a JavaScript variable that has not been defined yet.</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p>In most cases, searching <a href="https://forums.tumult.com">the forums</a> for the error you’re seeing will likely return helpful solutions. </p> 
     <p><strong>Reporting Bugs in the Application</strong></p> 
     <p>If you notice issues operating buttons, menus, or are experiencing issues specific to Tumult Hype, please <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/t/reporting-a-bug-within-hype/1550">submit a bug report</a>. Including your document and logs will help us find a solution for you quickly and potentially resolve the bug you’re reporting for everyone.</p> 
     <h2 id="hosting-amp-embedding">Hosting &amp; Embedding</h2> 
     <p>Please visit the <a href="#preview-amp-export">Exporting &amp; Previewing chapter</a> for help getting your document on the web or embedded elsewhere. For a list of guides covering how to embed Tumult Hype documents, visit <a href="https://forums.tumult.com/t/exporting-faq-guides-for-exporting-to-websites-apps-content-management-systems-and-more/799">this Exporting megapost</a>.</p> 
     <h1 id="version-history">Version History</h1>
     <h3 id="how-to-updatetumult-hype">How to Update&nbsp;Tumult Hype</h3> 
     <p><strong>Purchased through the Mac App Store</strong></p> 
     <p>If you purchased&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;through the Mac App Store, you can install the latest update by following these steps:</p> 
     <ol> 
      <li>Open the App Store by going to the Apple menu and selecting App Store</li> 
      <li>Click the Updates tab at the top of the App Store window</li> 
      <li>Tumult Hype&nbsp;should be listed in the Updates section, and clicking the Update button will install the latest update for free.</li> 
     </ol> 
     <p>If&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;isn’t listed in the Updates section, it’s either not installed at all or the latest version is already installed. If you are having issues, please try restarting your computer and signing out of the App Store application. Then, sign in again and check the Updates tab.</p> 
     <p><strong>Purchased through the Tumult Store</strong></p> 
     <p>If you purchased&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;through the&nbsp;<a href="http://tumult.com/store/">Tumult Store</a>, you can install the latest update by following these steps:</p> 
     <ol> 
      <li>Launch&nbsp;Tumult Hype</li> 
      <li>Select the Check for Updates menu item under the Hype menu</li> 
     </ol> 
     <p><a href="http://tumult.com/hype/purchasing/">Learn about purchasing&nbsp;Tumult Hype</a></p>

     <h3 id="detailed-release-notes">Detailed Release Notes</h3> 
     <p><a name="3.6.3"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="3-6-3---may-9th-2017">3.6.3 - May 9th, 2017</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Scenes/Layouts with the same size use the same zoom factor</li> 
      <li>Export Script options override choices from Advanced Export</li> 
      <li>Performance improvements to manipulating multiple resources in the Resource Library</li> 
      <li>Scroll position is better preserved when manipulating Resource Library</li> 
      <li>Cancelable GIF and APNG export in the final stage</li> 
      <li>Improvements to Layout API in-app documentation</li> 
      <li>Remove duplicate IE entries in cache.manifest file</li> 
      <li>Fix case where renaming *_hype_generated_script.js in a particular way could fail loading</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where actions are triggered twice by a Persistent Symbol in a group</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where newly created motion paths in a Symbol could export with an old version of the path</li> 
      <li>Fix case where flexible grouped elements within a hidden group may not appear when the group becomes visible</li> 
      <li>Resolved issue where editing a Custom CSS font may edit a different font</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where Inner HTML could be pasted on Persistent Symbols and break exporting</li> 
      <li>Crash fixes</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="3.6.2"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="3-6-2---april-5th-2017">3.6.2 - April 5th, 2017</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Fixes issue with audio not playing on iOS 10.3 (re-export required!)</li> 
      <li>Corrects issues exporting Animated GIF and PNGs on older versions of macOS</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where Animated GIFs with background transparency could show previous frames</li> 
      <li>Tabs will magnify when mousing over</li> 
      <li>Dragging multiple assets from the Resources Library won’t create extra copies anymore</li> 
      <li>JavaScript API callback for “HypeResourceLoad”</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="3.6.1"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="3-6-1---march-2nd-2017">3.6.1 - March 2nd, 2017</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Fix hang for Mac App Store version with Export Scripts</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="3.6.0"></a></p> 
     <h2 id="3-6-0---march-2nd-2017">3.6.0 - March 2nd, 2017</h2> 
     <ul> 
      <li>[PRO] Export Scripts extend Hype and improve export-based workflows</li> 
      <li>Animated GIF export quality is dramatically improved and file size reduced</li> 
      <li>Autoplay and inline video options for iOS 10+</li> 
      <li>Multiple selection in Resource Library</li> 
      <li>[PRO] Video export bitrate and codec settings</li> 
      <li>Removed Dropbox export since they are stopping public web serving</li> 
      <li>[PRO] Animated PNG export for iMessage Stickers</li> 
      <li>iMessage Sticker default scene sizes</li> 
      <li>Distributing app download as .dmg</li> 
      <li>Preference to change code editor font and size</li> 
      <li>Custom CSS Fonts are now re-editable</li> 
      <li>Groups preserve their expansion state when entering/exiting a symbol</li> 
      <li>Entering a low opacity or hidden symbol will now reveal it for editing</li> 
      <li>Improved accessibility aria tagging, especially for iOS navigation</li> 
      <li>Zoom scene editor down to 10%</li> 
      <li>Zoom level is per-scene/layout</li> 
      <li>Microsoft Edge browser warnings and runtime support</li> 
      <li>Asks to replace files with the same name dragged into the Resource Library</li> 
      <li>Movie exports remember manually entered time duration</li> 
      <li>APIs/callbacks for manipulating Layouts</li> 
      <li>JavaScript notifications for HypeSymbolLoad and HypeSymbolUnload events</li> 
      <li>JavaScript setter API allows changing background-image</li> 
      <li>When adding a new font, the current selected elements will use that font</li> 
      <li>Removed WAV slot from audio</li> 
      <li>Accessibility tab-index UI is simplified</li> 
      <li>Smoother animation (position and scaling) for IE 10+ and Edge</li> 
      <li>Simplified group dot drawing</li> 
      <li>Elements on top of symbol no longer interfere with selection</li> 
      <li>Improved app editing performance on Late 2016 MacBook Pros using P3/Wide gamut color profiles</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where undoing group resize from top or left doesn’t move the children back</li> 
      <li>Fixed multiple issues running symbols in reverse</li> 
      <li>Fixed issues where symbol state was not properly synced with parent timeline playhead</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where Symbol action that starts a timeline does not respect relative values</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where Custom behavior handlers of a symbol in a persistent symbol stop working on a scene - change</li> 
      <li>On Drag to control a timeline will play the last timeline action if dragged to the end</li> 
      <li>Better velocity for continuing a timeline after a drag</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where drag to control timeline would not continue properly if the drag was slower than - timeline speed</li> 
      <li>In-App feedback attempts to preserve name/email or warn if it is not being sent</li> 
      <li>Control/right-clicking will not trigger mouse actions</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where audio would stop working on Chrome when there are more than 6 Hype animations on a page</li> 
      <li>Fixed a bug where duplicating scene removes the layout grid on the original scene</li> 
      <li>Reduced cases where copying animations could result in duplicate custom timing functions</li> 
      <li>Properly copy custom timing functions across documents</li> 
      <li>Improved JavaScript runtime performance loading a scene with many nested flexible layout groups</li> 
      <li>Improved JavaScript runtime performance when there are a lot of active timelines</li> 
      <li>Improved JavaScript runtime frame rate on iOS</li> 
      <li>Reduced MSIE 6-9 code not necessary in the thin JavaScript runtime</li> 
      <li>Updating mechanism is better at checking in the face of Gatekeeper Path Randomization</li> 
      <li>Sierra: Fix double-selection for timing functions</li> 
      <li>Sierra: Fix bug where resource library disclosure triangles do not close</li> 
      <li>Sierra: Potentially fixed issue causing corrupt video exports</li> 
      <li>Drag with Control Element Position offsets appropriately with parent’s Zoom Contents Flexible Layout option</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where an element with scale zoom contents and a non 50%/50% transform origin is off on scene - changes</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where checking create enclosing folder in Advanced Export can clear Use External Runtime URL field</li> 
      <li>Zoom Contents checkbox is colored correctly in 10.8 with Pro theme</li> 
      <li>OAM Widgets with transparent backgrounds show up that way in Muse’s editor</li> 
      <li>Hidden default for disabling color picker as a popover window (useColorPickerPopOver)</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug from selecting multiple videos</li> 
      <li>Constrain ratio math for scaling handles 0% values better</li> 
      <li>Opacity no longer displayed for scene background color</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where moving keyframes with motion paths via arrow keys would jump further than expected amount</li> 
      <li>Advanced Export uses the first scene in the slice as the document size instead of the absolute first scene</li> 
      <li>Does not write out duplicate iframe html files to reduce export size</li> 
      <li>Improved Italian localization for breakpoint</li> 
      <li>Fix hang caused by pasting specific elements</li> 
      <li>Fixed crashes </li> 
     </ul>

     <p>For more details and a tutorial video, please see&nbsp;<a href="http://tumult.com/hype/whats-new/2.0/">What’s New In&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;2.0</a>.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Instant previews to iOS with&nbsp;<a href="http://tumult.com/hype/reflect/">Hype Reflect</a></li> 
      <li>Audio actions</li> 
      <li>Curved Motion Paths</li> 
      <li>Google Fonts and custom web fonts</li> 
      <li>Scene-level Swipe left/right/up/down events</li> 
      <li>Element and scene-level drag events</li> 
      <li>Touch and tap handlers joined with mouse action handlers</li> 
      <li>iOS web app support</li> 
      <li>Option to hide iOS location bar on page load</li> 
      <li>Option to prevent iOS tap highlighting</li> 
      <li>Support for offline web content using cache manifest file</li> 
      <li>Preview toolbar button now offers a list of all browsers and devices running&nbsp;Hype Reflect</li> 
      <li>Search engine support with option to export text contents</li> 
      <li>Added two new shapes — circle and rounded rectangle</li> 
      <li>Renamed “Box” to Rectangle for consistency</li> 
      <li>Quick Look support</li> 
      <li>Full Screen support</li> 
      <li>Spotlight support</li> 
      <li>Introduced a new JavaScript API to get the id of the exported document’s container div:&nbsp;<code class="prettyprint">hypeDocument.documentId()</code></li> 
      <li>Double clicking a function’s or variable’s row in the documentation viewer inserts the function or variable</li> 
      <li>Added a View &gt; Center on Scene command, to quickly center&nbsp;Tumult Hype’s&nbsp;scene editor on the scene itself</li> 
      <li>Better rotation control in Metrics inspector which now handles counter-clockwise rotation in addition to clockwise.</li> 
      <li>Multiple elements can now be rotated in the scene editor by selecting multiple elements and command-dragging on a selected element’s corner resize handle</li> 
      <li>Support for Opera 15</li> 
      <li>Browser compatibility data has been updated for the latest browsers</li> 
      <li>iOS 5’s Safari is now the minimum browser for Mobile Safari warnings</li> 
      <li>By default, only common browsers will be shown as choices in preview menus; this behavior can be toggled by a new “Only show recommended browsers in preview menu” option in Tumult Hype’s preferences</li> 
      <li>Scene transitions have been completely rewritten; the new system avoids gaps in Push transitions and all transitions are now more consistent across browsers</li> 
      <li>Unlicensed copies of&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;2.0 warn about upgrading when opening 1.x documents</li> 
      <li>Anonymous usage reporting has been enabled; data is only submitted if the user has explicitly agreed</li> 
      <li>Tumult Hype 2’s “bundle identifier” has been changed from&nbsp;<code class="prettyprint">com.tumult.Hype</code>&nbsp;to&nbsp;<code class="prettyprint">com.tumult.Hype2</code></li> 
      <li>Fixed many common crashes</li> 
      <li>Resolved issue where YouTube videos would not display properly or work with iBooks Author documents</li> 
      <li>Insulates custom JavaScript so if there are errors it won’t interfere with the timeline</li> 
      <li>Pressing Enter while completing kanji no longer clears the text in inner HTML editor</li> 
      <li>Transparent PNGs now work on IE 6, and no longer render incorrectly on IE 7</li> 
      <li>Custom keyboard shortcuts broken on Lion when sandboxed (must quit and relaunch for custom keyboard shortcut changes to be noticed)</li> 
      <li>The Brightness CSS Filter now works properly in Chrome</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where CSS3 Filter Effect Brightness could be applied incorrectly when using Safari Seed</li> 
      <li>Guide creator dialog is incorrectly sized on first open</li> 
      <li>Now scrolls to the appropriate item after choosing Reveal in Resource Library</li> 
      <li>Animated GIFs now animate in documents that have been exported to Dropbox</li> 
      <li>CSS Filter Effect controls have been moved to the bottom of the Element inspector</li> 
      <li>The Media Browser is better behaved with multiple spaces, and with Full Screen</li> 
      <li>Warn that TIFF and PSD images don’t render in most browsers</li> 
      <li>No longer incorrectly warn that iBooks doesn’t support CSS Filters</li> 
      <li>No longer incorrectly warn about video incompatibilities for image elements</li> 
      <li>Video warnings now have a correct category warning</li> 
      <li>Mouse events work properly in IE 9 when the document is in “quirks mode”</li> 
      <li>Opacity is now animated under IE 9 when the document is in “quirks mode”</li> 
      <li>Fixed an issue where setting and unsetting the blur CSS Filter Effect would cause images to remain blurry</li> 
      <li>Buttons without a fill, with no background image, or with a transparent fill color now behave properly on IE 6 through IE 8</li> 
      <li>No longer incorrectly warn about SVG incompatibility with IE 9</li> 
      <li>Prevent videos from being replaced with images, and vice versa</li> 
      <li>Fixed a case where a text element’s background color would be drawn outside of the element’s bounds</li>
