     <p><a name="1.6.0"></a></p> 
     <h2 id="1-6-0---january-7-2013">1.6.0 - January 7, 2013</h2> 
     <p>For more details and a tutorial video, please see&nbsp;<a href="http://tumult.com/hype/whats-new/1.6/">What’s New In&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;1.6</a>.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Support for CSS Filter Effects&nbsp;<em>(requires Safari 6 to be installed)</em></li> 
      <li>Resource Library for managing images, videos, functions, and document assets</li> 
      <li>Capo: create arbitrary animation start times</li> 
      <li>Layout guides to a scene in bulk, defining either a distance between or a number of guides</li> 
      <li>Retina artwork and icons in the application</li> 
      <li>Tumult Hype&nbsp;is now Sandboxed</li> 
      <li>New actions to pause, continue, and jump to specific times</li> 
      <li>Timeline Actions which can be triggered at any point on the timeline</li> 
      <li>Action chaining to make sophisticated flows</li> 
      <li>The document’s HTML &lt;head&gt; contents can now be modified</li> 
      <li>Preloading of images can now be toggled via the Resource Library</li> 
      <li>Support for IE10 3D transforms and gradients</li> 
      <li>More iOS-supported fonts in the font panel</li> 
      <li>Timelines can now be set to have absolute or relative initial keyframes</li> 
      <li>Absolute keyframes, rather than relative keyframes, are now the default for new timelines</li> 
      <li>Reduce HYPE.js size to 38.08 KB (279 bytes less than 1.5.2!)</li> 
      <li>API Documentation Viewer for Javascript and &lt;head&gt; editors</li> 
      <li>Syntax highlighting for Javascript and CSS within HTML</li> 
      <li>JavaScript APIs for starting, pausing, and continuing timelines, as well as jumping to a specific time on a timeline</li> 
      <li>JavaScript API for invoking custom JavaScript functions written in&nbsp;Tumult Hype</li> 
      <li>JavaScript API for getting the URL of the document’s associated resources folder</li> 
      <li>Added event.timelineName property to the On Animation Complete javascript callback to determine which was completed</li> 
      <li>External scripts can now register for callbacks on HypeDocumentLoad / HypeSceneLoad / HypeSceneUnload /HypeTimelineComplete events</li> 
      <li>Identical&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;documents can now be loaded in the same HTML page</li> 
      <li>Find/Replace support for&nbsp;Tumult Hype’s JavaScript editor</li> 
      <li>Indent/Outdent keyboard shortcuts for JavaScript editing</li> 
      <li>Browser warnings are now defined by a minimum version number or ‘none’, rather than discrete checkboxes, per browser</li> 
      <li>Rotate elements on their z-axis by command clicking on a corner resize point and dragging</li> 
      <li>With multiple elements selected, resizing one will proportionally resize all other selected elements</li> 
      <li>Option to enable/disable webkit graphics acceleration in Document Inspector</li> 
      <li>Generates iBooks Author/Dashboard widget thumbnail from the current scene and time</li> 
      <li>Generates retina @2x thumbnails for iBooks Author/Dashboard widgets</li> 
      <li>Browser compatibility warnings for iBooks 3</li> 
      <li>Show and hide user created guides</li> 
      <li>Command-clicking lock/visibility will toggle all, option-clicking will toggle others</li> 
      <li>Previews are now handled via a built-in server, rather than via exported files</li> 
      <li>During editing, text elements now respect the selected text’s justification when resizing (e.g. right justified text will cause the text element to resize from the left)</li> 
      <li>Pressing the Escape key while editing an element will end editing</li> 
      <li>Keyframes can now be stacked, when animations overlap on the timeline and represents an instant transition</li> 
      <li>Multiple animations or keyframes can be selected via shift clicking</li> 
      <li>Way to have extended trials</li> 
      <li>“Play Timeline” action has been renamed to “Start Timeline”</li> 
      <li>“On Animation Complete” has been renamed to “On Timeline Complete”</li> 
      <li>“Use Vertical Layout” has been renamed to “Widescreen Layout”</li> 
      <li>Document resource folder name is now “documentName”.resources rather than “documentName”_Resources</li> 
      <li>Show Guides menu item is now in the Arrange &gt; Guides submenu</li> 
      <li>Arrange &gt; Align menu items have been renamed and rearranged for clarity</li> 
      <li>Added document sizes for iPad 3 and iPhone 5</li> 
      <li>Does not have the “Build with Hype” watermark enabled by default</li> 
      <li>The “Built With Hype” now opens http://tumult.com/hype/ in a new browser window</li> 
      <li>Fixed nasty bug where resources might go missing</li> 
      <li>IE 10 and other current browser compatibility updates</li> 
      <li>Aliases to images and videos are now resolved to the source file when added to a document</li> 
      <li>Animation segments in the element list can now be resized such that all associated animations are reversed</li> 
      <li>Changes made in the inspector are now applied before changing scenes</li> 
      <li>Documents with a ‘.’ in their name will now preview with the correct name</li> 
      <li>Documents with a space at the end of their file name can now be uploaded to Dropbox</li> 
      <li>Duplicating an element nested in a group will create the new element in the same group</li> 
      <li>Elements with invalid origins or sizes will no longer prevent documents from being edited</li> 
      <li>Elements with zero width and/or height are better handled</li> 
      <li>Fixed a case where the selected element may not be highlighted in the element list</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue causing text elements to wrap when being edited near the scene bounds</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where button states could be displayed incorrectly</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where guides would always be locked even if no guides are present, preventing any new guides from being added</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where identically named timelines would prevent any timeline other than the first such named timeline from being edited</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where moving elements into or out of groups could lead to incorrect z-ordering</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where playing the main timeline on scene load could lead to issues when transitioning to other scenes</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where pressing the spacebar while editing an HTML Widget would play or pause playback rather than insert a space</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where scene would not properly update if an edited element’s text scrolled past the bottom of the visible window</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where the Format &gt; Font &gt; Bigger/Smaller might not have any effect</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where videos could be incorrectly positioned on IE 8 and earlier</li> 
      <li>Fixed issues where Inspector could take focus, losing changes to text elements, or preventing keyboard commands (such as playing and pausing using the space bar) from being honored by the scene editor</li> 
      <li>Fixed some cases where images would flicker after a scene change on Chrome and Safari 6</li> 
      <li>Fixed some cases where the scene border would be drawn incorrectly after launching&nbsp;Tumult Hype</li> 
      <li>Generate Dashboard and iBooks Author Widget thumbnails at the correct pixel size</li> 
      <li>Tumult Hype&nbsp;quits more quickly</li> 
      <li>Shows reflections during scene transitions</li> 
      <li>Scene selector will no longer have focus after a change has been made</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where the scene would redraw/flicker when recording animations</li> 
      <li>Properly preserve nesting when making groups</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where pasted text would wrongly resize together</li> 
      <li>Does not allow elements/groups in hidden groups to be selected</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where undo would not work correctly when moving keyframes</li> 
      <li>Trebuchet MS will now display in Firefox and IE</li> 
      <li>Do not allow timing functions to change on locked elements</li> 
      <li>Properly sandbox margin-left for li in CSS Reset</li> 
      <li>IE6-8 video elements (using quicktime plugin) will pause on scene unload</li> 
      <li>Fixed several crashers</li> 
      <li>Does not warn about text-shadow for IE10 as it supports it</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where grouped elements will look bad on Retina macs within&nbsp;Tumult Hype</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where ‘open in window’ would not work on iOS webapps</li> 
      <li>Fix bug where animations can be resized to a time less than zero</li> 
      <li>Command-clicking on links will now open in a new tab for some browsers</li> 
      <li>Correctly use iBooks Author document sizes</li> 
      <li>Better warning for iOS 6 autoplaying</li> 
      <li>Improved guideline hit detection and snapping for cases when many guides are close together</li> 
      <li>Improved timeline resize behavior when moving keyframes or animation segments at the end of the timeline</li> 
      <li>It’s now possible to undo the deletion of video elements with multiple sources</li> 
      <li>Line height can now always be modified, even if the element already has multiple line heights defined</li> 
      <li>Made element resize handles easier to click and drag</li> 
      <li>Many issues around dragging multiple animations and/or keyframes have been resolved</li> 
      <li>New documents respect ruler visibility changes made with earlier documents</li> 
      <li>Pasting content when a button is in a state other than “Normal” now works properly</li> 
      <li>Popovers are now dismissed when their associated document window is closed</li> 
      <li>Removing all guides will now remove guides that covered each other</li> 
      <li>Resizing proportionally constrained elements past scene bounds no longer causes erratic element movement</li> 
      <li>Text Spacing can now be set back to “Auto” after having been set to a different value</li> 
      <li>Text shadow offsets can now have negative values</li> 
      <li>The loop button’s state is now properly preserved after changing scenes</li> 
      <li>The playhead will now remain visible when moved with keyboard shortcuts, even if it moves beyond the timeline’s current visible bounds</li> 
      <li>When resizing an element nested in a group, resize guides are now drawn correctly</li> 
      <li>Many top crashes have been fixed</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.5.2"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="1-5-2---september-20-2012">1.5.2 - September 20, 2012</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Mountain Lion minor fixes</li> 
      <li>Command-clicking lock/visibility will toggle all, option-clicking will toggle others</li> 
      <li>Added event.timelineName property to the On Animation Complete javascript callback to determine which was completed</li> 
      <li>Workaround for issue where Chrome and now Safari 6 images would flicker when using Dropbox</li> 
      <li>Improved element placement on IE6-8</li> 
      <li>Fixed issues where z-index may be incorrect inside groups</li> 
      <li>Improved scrolling on iOS for the HTML Widget</li> 
      <li>Fixed top crasher that could occur when closing documents with videos</li> 
      <li>Fixed an 1.5.0 regression where button states might display incorrectly</li> 
      <li>Fixed an issue where a crash could occur when resizing the document</li> 
      <li>Updated to latest Dropbox SDK which handles /public folder deprecation</li> 
      <li>Properly generates thumbnail images on Retina Macs for iBooks Author</li> 
      <li>Hang reporting mechanism</li> 
      <li>Better focus behavior for the inspector</li> 
      <li>Quits faster</li> 
      <li>Fixes issue where sometimes the spacebar could not be used to pause</li> 
      <li>Better handles adding alias files</li> 
      <li>Keyboard shortcuts for moving playhead will also scroll the view when necessary</li> 
      <li>Improved ability to resize/move animations near the end of the timeline</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where duplicating an element in a group would make the duplicate outside the group</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where playing the main timeline on scene load could lead to wonkiness when transitioning to other scenes</li> 
      <li>Does not show the iframe border in IE7-8</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.5.1"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="1-5-1---may-9-2012">1.5.1 - May 9, 2012</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Copy/Paste Scenes</li> 
      <li>Option-clicking the keyframe button will add keyframes for every visible property on selected elements</li> 
      <li>Attachments can now be added to feedback reporter</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where rotated elements would not show up correctly in IE</li> 
      <li>Restored v1.0.x’s rotateY(0deg) trick for performance improvements</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where scenes might not be able to be duplicated</li> 
      <li>Animations in groups are now pasted correctly</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where overlapping elements might not be able to move</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where 0px by 0px elements (like audio) would eat mouse selection</li> 
      <li>Faster loading on IE9 for documents with lots of images</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where jQuery could interfere with&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;animations</li> 
      <li>Reverting will correctly revert open JavaScripts</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where scrollbars could not be dragged when ruler is visible</li> 
      <li>Resolved issue where locked guides would not allow elements to be moved</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where double-clicking rulers would change the document layout</li> 
      <li>Locking disallows mouse action manipulation</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where swap transitions would show elements outside of scene</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where missing fonts could lead to not being able to edit Javascript/InnerHTML</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.5.0"></a></p> 
     <h2 id="1-5-0---february-23-2012">1.5.0 - February 23, 2012</h2> 
     <p>For more details and a tutorial video, please see&nbsp;<a href="http://tumult.com/hype/whats-new/1.5/">What’s New In&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;1.5</a>.</p> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Redesigned animation interface separating element and keyframe editing</li> 
      <li>Grouping</li> 
      <li>Scene zooming</li> 
      <li>Element locking and visibility toggles</li> 
      <li>Improved Lion support (Versions, Autosave, Scrolling)</li> 
      <li>‘Export as HTML5 &gt; Dashboard/iBooks Author Widget’</li> 
      <li>Rulers</li> 
      <li>Custom Guidelines</li> 
      <li>“Paste with Animations” for element copying</li> 
      <li>Bounce and instant animation timing functions</li> 
      <li>Insert “HTML Widget” for arbitrary code/script execution</li> 
      <li>Exported Javascript is significantly smaller (generally 1/3 the size of 1.0.5; a minimal document only requires 41 KB download)</li> 
      <li>New app icon</li> 
      <li>Can change window layout to have vertical timelines on the right</li> 
      <li>Accurate motion paths when selecting elements</li> 
      <li>Hex color picker</li> 
      <li>Compose email action</li> 
      <li>Context menus throughout the application</li> 
      <li>Improved selection behavior so selections made in the element list are preserved</li> 
      <li>3D support for Firefox 10</li> 
      <li>Updated supported browser list/warnings</li> 
      <li>Selection colors better show which view is active</li> 
      <li>Relative element spacing and sizing snapping</li> 
      <li>Editable Timecode/Go to Time (command-shift-t)</li> 
      <li>Ability to set your own ids on elements</li> 
      <li>Custom javascript functions now get the triggering event</li> 
      <li>Easier to adjust items at the end of a timeline</li> 
      <li>Document default sizes for mobile banner ads, iPhone retina displays, and iBooks Author Widgets</li> 
      <li>Playhead does not cover timeline (ticks reversed)</li> 
      <li>Malformed javascript no longer kills the page</li> 
      <li>hypeDocument.getElementById() API added</li> 
      <li>Can run &lt;script&gt; if there’s no source in innerHTML</li> 
      <li>Top-level HYPE object is now versioned to avoid conflicts</li> 
      <li>Adopted window.requestAnimationFrame for better browser performance</li> 
      <li>Push and Crossfade scene transitions for more browsers</li> 
      <li>Context menu item to refresh inner html content</li> 
      <li>Rearranged menu items (preview is now in the File menu)</li> 
      <li>New keyboard shortcuts for exporting, animation navigation</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where Save/Save As would not work complaining “File exists”</li> 
      <li>Worked around IE issue where IE6 would report “Stack Overflow on Line 0”</li> 
      <li>Worked around Safari issue where rotated elements would not be animated correctly</li> 
      <li>Worked around Safari issue where full screen videos would not display properly</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where background color for elements may be unable to be changed</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where the color picker’s colors would not match</li> 
      <li>Removed CSS3 Transitions and forced hardware compositing</li> 
      <li>Resource tracking is better about notifying for changes on launch</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where the spacebar would sometimes stop working for playing</li> 
      <li>Worked around IE issue where it doesn’t always capture mouse events when background fill style is none</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where videos could appear blank</li> 
      <li>Less renaming (Image-1, Image-2) of resources</li> 
      <li>Fixed console warnings in Firefox about parentElement</li> 
      <li>If an image is changed outside of&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;and then adopted, the “original size” value is now updated</li> 
      <li>Scene duplication will add a scene after the currently selected scene</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where mouseout events could happen from the wrong scene</li> 
      <li>Original width/height now update when choosing a new background image</li> 
      <li>Properly updates element position when changing timing functions</li> 
      <li>Workaround potential issue where timecode view font can’t load</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where element may not rotate in exported version if rotation animation was copied to the element</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where playTimeline() API would not work on scene load</li> 
      <li>Disable Mac OS X’s automatic text substitutions</li> 
      <li>Fixed graphics glitch when scrolling javascript on Lion</li> 
      <li>Fixed issues with scene thumbnail drawing</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where Inner HTML editor may disappear</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where animation configuration might not be displayed on screen</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where deleting the last bracket in a function would not let you add it back</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where content was not completely sandboxed from rest of page in Firefox</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where button may not show accurately on different timelines</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where a text shadow of 0px 0px was still showing a small shadow</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where changing scenes during a scene change could lead to the wrong/blank scene</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where items could be randomly selected after deleting elements</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where animation popover would be in the wrong place after a scroll</li> 
      <li>Fixed data loss where changing a timeline would discard inner html edits</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where export warning dialog window could be improperly sized</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where editing javascript did not reflect in the document being modified</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where editing the animation timing function did not reflect in the document being modified</li> 
      <li>Improved timeline execution performance</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where feedback reporter dialog would be on top of other application windows</li> 
      <li>Fixed feedback reporter window sizing issues</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where text spacing controls would show fractions</li> 
      <li>Fixed element placement</li> 
      <li>Removed print toolbar button</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where the preference pane may be highlighting the wrong view</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where saving a document while editing inner html would not result in the inner html being saved</li> 
      <li>Many performance improvements</li> 
      <li>Fixed other crashers</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.0.5"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="1-0-5---september-1-2011">1.0.5 - September 1, 2011</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Fixed 1.0.4 regression where key action handlers could cause the document to be blank on export</li> 
      <li>More Lion Fixes</li> 
      <li>Resolved issue where video elements could appear blank on launch</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where border stroke colors might not be set properly</li> 
      <li>Fixed bug where dragging and dropping in the element list could result in the wrong z-index</li> 
      <li>Better support for special characters in resources</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.0.4"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="1-0-4---august-7-2011">1.0.4 - August 7, 2011</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>14-day full trial support</li> 
      <li>Non Mac App Store purchasing option</li> 
      <li>Radial snapping when holding the shift key while dragging</li> 
      <li>Fixed color picker glitches for background color with HSV/CMYK/different profiles</li> 
      <li>Copy/Pasting preserves z-ordering of elements</li> 
      <li>Fix some cases where resources aren’t being deleted</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where button images could get stuck in the hover state for IE</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where rotation would be offset in IE 6-8</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where video would sometimes not play on IE 6-8</li> 
      <li>Duplicating a scene will duplicate scene actions</li> 
      <li>Force utilizing hardware acceleration</li> 
      <li>Setting an image in the element inspector will unset the background color</li> 
      <li>Faster performance and less jittering when playing back with large elements</li> 
      <li>Lion fixes</li> 
      <li>Open URL action now will break out of iframes</li> 
      <li>Performance improvements when opening/previewing large documents</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where element editor could be shown over JavaScripts</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where X or Y rotations could cause Z rotations in Firefox</li> 
      <li>Do not allow interaction with iframes in the scene editor</li> 
      <li>Fixed crasher when playing or changing scenes and closing the document</li> 
      <li>Shows warnings for scene actions</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where changing shadow color could also change text color</li> 
      <li>Workaround for all text not being selected when entering edit mode with Safari 5.1</li> 
      <li>Updated to latest iMedia Browser Framework</li> 
      <li>Resolved issue where HYPE.js could be loaded multiple times</li> 
      <li>Removed border from iframe CSS reset</li> 
      <li>HYPE.documents properly lists all&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;embeds on the page</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where keypress handlers would not be removed</li> 
      <li>Re-initialize dropbox sheet for each export</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where documents would not save if a timeline was undone</li> 
      <li>Fixed Lion scroller issue</li> 
      <li>Fix issue where public API doesn’t expose kSceneTransitionPushRightToLeft</li> 
      <li>CSS Resets background-color appropriately</li> 
      <li>Does not allow editing before “function” in javascripts</li> 
      <li>Faster export time if warnings are turned off</li> 
      <li>Many other misc. fixes</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.0.3"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="1-0-3---june-14-2011">1.0.3 - June 14, 2011</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Implemented Revert to Saved</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where buttons could not be clicked on their text</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue with images not working in iframes for IE/Firefox only</li> 
      <li>PNGs in IE look much better</li> 
      <li>Fixed crash/hang when trying to look for resources on unreachable servers</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where some characters could cause parse errors for the JSON</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where negative widths/heights could cause animation to behave unexpectedly</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue not being able to duplicate scenes from an older version</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where timelines could not run at scene load/unload time</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where Dreamweaver could kill&nbsp;Tumult Hype’s output</li> 
      <li>If text is 100% opaque, don’t use alpha filter so it looks better in IE</li> 
      <li>Remove shadow and reflection if not actually used</li> 
      <li>Remove mouse actions if not actually used</li> 
      <li>Fix video on next big cat</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.0.2"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="1-0-2---may-31-2011">1.0.2 - May 31, 2011</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Show “Built with Hype” can additionally be found in general preferences</li> 
      <li>Fixed regression saving when duplicating scenes without animations</li> 
      <li>Fixed issues with the next big cat</li> 
      <li>Fixed color picker issue where colors won’t apply</li> 
      <li>Fixed crash on close for the feedback reporter</li> 
      <li>Other misc. fixes</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.0.1"></a></p> 
     <h3 id="1-0-1---may-27-2011">1.0.1 - May 27, 2011</h3> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Easier separation between HTML and Resources (you only need to edit the script tag’s src in the HTML)</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue where the preview/export could be blank</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue with deleting duplicated scenes using buttons</li> 
      <li>Fixed issue preventing&nbsp;Tumult Hype&nbsp;documents from being embedded in iframes</li> 
      <li>Fixed text shadows not always showing up for buttons</li> 
     </ul> 
     <p><a name="1.0.0"></a></p> 
     <h2 id="1-0-0---may-20-2011">1.0.0 - May 20, 2011</h2> 
     <ul> 
      <li>Initial Release</li> 
     </ul>
